<h1>The Radical Forest</h1> <img src="https://images.pexels.com/photos/1690355/pexels-photo-1690355.jpeg" width="500"> <span style="font-size: w00px; font-weight: bold;">Welcome to the Radical Forest</span> You're an awful ways away from home. Did you mean to come here? [[Yes, let us begin.|Begin]] [[No, I'll just turn around now...]] ah ah ah! [[Too late.|Begin]]''This journey begins just as any other, quiet and calm...'' <img src="https://media.istockphoto.com/id/690192102/photo/two-road-in-forest.jpg?s=612x612&w=0&k=20&c=PkXt_vjwcVqKZVffHO3AcSeD2ff_RfuHXDMSjlURTQc= " width="500"> ...that is, until you are suddenly confronted by the forking of two paths! You notice to your left, that the path seems much more pleasant, and full of color. You notice to the right, that the path is a lot more gray, with a gloomier feel. Where do you proceed, traveler? [[Let's go left]] [[Let's go right|You can't go wrong when you go right!]]''Oh my! What's this?'' <img src="https://i.etsystatic.com/26650952/r/il/2d6da9/6030932150/il_1080xN.6030932150_d5fc.jpg" width="500"> It seems you have come across your first treasure, and early too! [[Let's open it!]] [[Nah, this is too early... seems sus.]]''Alright, let's go right'' As you begin your jouney, you notice that the further you go this path, the darker it seems to be. It seems that the once lively and vibrant aura of the forest left with haste. Even your footsteps made no noise as you ran. [[Continue]]''Oh no, its a mimic!'' <img src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/forgottenrealms/images/5/59/Mimic-5e.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200410111521" width="500"> Treasure this early *did* feel a bit suspicious... GAME OVER [[RESTART|Begin]] ''That was definitely a trap, right?'' Oh well. Trap or not, you decide to leave the chest behind, and continue your journey. <img src="https://images.fineartamerica.com/images-medium-large-5/forest-path-bob-van-den-berg-photography.jpg" width="500"> As you continue to make your way through the forest, you begin to hear a sound from afar. "Hey! Heeeeey! Come to me, young and brave traveler!" [[Let's go see who's calling|Let's go see whos calling for me!]]<img src="https://www.zbrushcentral.com/uploads/default/original/4X/0/0/1/001e2ac5dff6bdff4ccdd8dc85dd78906884d9f5.jpeg" width="500"> ''Traveler, oh traveler! '' You wish to reach the end of the forest, do you not? Well, I can help you get there! But you must solve a riddle! What do you say? [[Alright, what is your riddle?]] [[No, I'll find the exit on my own.]]''Good choice, traveler! Now, for your riddle...'' I’m taken before you need me, I’m given when you use me, And once you use me, I’m gone. What am I? [[A match.]] [[A photograph.]]''Oh. Find yourself above my challenge, do you?!'' <img src="https://pbs.twimg.com/profile_images/997924093574828032/LjCDBJab_400x400.jpg" width="500"> "You must now defeat me, or you will be stuck in this forest FOREVER!" [[Accept Duel]] ''You accept the duel.'' But how do you defeat an all-powerful wizard? Maybe you should have listened to that riddle after all.. What do you do? Alright, I yield! I'll [[listen to your riddle.|Alright, what is your riddle?]] No, I *hate* riddles! I'll [[fight the wizard.]]''"INCORRECT!"'' <img src="https://images.pond5.com/4k-wizard-laughing-hysterically-green-footage-045785053_iconl.jpeg " width="500"> Though your answer was not correct, the wizard still seems amused. "You may have been wrong, but I am glad that you decided to listen to my riddle anyways. If you wish to exit the forrest, you must find the ''silent giant of the woods.''" The "silent giant of the woods"? Of course! that must mean: the [[Elder Bear Norkaur]], he can lead me to the exit! the [[Wise and Ancient Tree Eldorum]], it is where the exit lies! ''"CORRECT"'' <img src="https://images.pond5.com/4k-wizard-laughing-hysterically-green-footage-045785053_iconl.jpeg " width="500"> The wizard is very pleased to hear the correct answer to his riddle, and tells you a way to get to the exit happily. "You wish to leave, don't you? Then you must speak with the [[Wise and Ancient Tree Eldorum]], for he is the guardian of the forrest gate! ''"Foolish traveler!"'' <img src="https://pbs.twimg.com/profile_images/997924093574828032/LjCDBJab_400x400.jpg" width="500"> "Did you *really* think that you could ever beat *me*?!" The wizard simply points his staff at you, and you turn into a pile of dust. width="500"> What were once the friendly unmvoing trees of the radical forest have suddenly started moving, creeping towards you! You aren't able to go anywhere except forward. [[Continue foward]] ''You call out to the forest...'' Something answers... It sounds like *you*! Do you go towards the sound? [[Investigate the familair sound]] [[Keep walking]]''There's no going back now, you chose your fate.'' <img src="https://i.ytimg.com/vi/_4ekAX7YGiQ/hq720.jpg?sqp=-oaymwEhCK4FEIIDSFryq4qpAxMIARUAAAAAGAElAADIQj0AgKJD&rs=AOn4CLD-hz4wBLpvYFwctJL9CZGXZrrSrw" width="500"> The forest insists you continue forward. [[Continue ahead||Keep walking]] ''As you walk towards the sound, you notice something terrifying!'' <img src="https://i.etsystatic.com/7478392/r/il/8ffdeb/4534285100/il_fullxfull.4534285100_ip4d.jpg" width="500"> A tree, in the middle of the path, with a wooden carving of a person that looks just like you. You walk towards it, and notice a sign nearby that says "Welcome back." [[Look closer at the tree carving]] ''Is this the end?!'' <img src="https://c8.alamy.com/comp/2EAB0K5/oak-forest-in-winter-with-a-view-of-the-bottom-of-the-tree-canopy-some-oak-trees-are-heavily-overgrown-with-ivy-2EAB0K5.jpg" width="500"> You keep walking, and as you continue, the forest seems to grow larger and larger. The path narrows. The air feels thinner. The trees grow to be taller than buildings! Perhaps you should have investigated that sound earlier... Yeah, [[let's go see what that sound was about]] No, [[I'll see this to the end!]] You decide to run back to where you first heard that sound. The trees seem less crowded in this direction. Almost like they’re making room for you. [[Investigate the familair sound]]''You decide to keep going forward.'' <img src="https://www.shutterstock.com/shutterstock/videos/1107298445/thumb/1.jpg?ip=x480" width="500"> The trees get closer. Branches scrape against your shoulders. The forest grows darker. The sky vanishes above you. The sound does not follow. [[And then....]] The trees stop moving. The air returns to your lungs. The sky opens above you. The forest is no longer pressing in. It is simply… a forest. And ahead, you see the edge of it. [[You step out.]]''You survived!'' But... As you walk out, you notice that the forest is quiet. Too quiet. As you keep walking forward, a path stretches out before you. [[It splits in two.|Begin]]The carving is detailed. Too detailed. The shape of the eyes. The curve of the mouth. Even the small scar near your brow. You don’t remember ever standing this still. The forest around you is calm here. No wind. No movement. As if this place is protected. The wood around the carving looks softer than the rest of the bark. Warmer. Almost breathing. You could touch the carving. Or step back. [[Touch it.]] [[Step away.]]The wood is warm. Warmer than skin. Your hand does not pull away. It does not feel trapped. It feels… correct. The bark shifts gently. Your fingers sink into it as if into water. There is no pain. Only stillness. You have been walking for so long. It is nice to finally rest. The forest absorbs you, and you become one with it. GAME OVER [[RESTART|Begin]]''It's too late to run now.'' You take a step back. The path behind you is gone. The forest is quiet. The carving’s expression changes. It looks relieved. The carving smiles at you, and the words on the sign next to it shift: "Welcome home." GAME OVER [[RESTART|Begin]]
